<rating>5</rating><review>So many flavors of olive oil and balsamic vinegar! Too many for me to choose from, so I usually stick with my tried and true: Garlic infused.  The garlic flavor is very strong so if you're not a HUGE fan of garlic, ask for something a little more mild.

< review>
I had some time to kill while visiting Sacramento and decided to check out Old Town.  Many of the stores and restaurants were pretty touristy.  However I really liked this shop that sells fine balsalmic vinegars and EVOOs (extra virgin olive oils). I've  seen stores like this before but this one was particularly well designed with premiums products that you can sample before buying.

What really sets this one apart from others was the friendly, helpful staff.  The young lady that was working there that day greeted me at that door, asked if she could tell me about the store and happily answered my questions.

I cook often and have some very fine, imported vinegars and EVOOs from all over the world.  Their selections were delicious and a great value for what it is.  I won't stop buying the really expensive, Italian aged Balsamic Vinegar for the rare gourmet gatherings that I attend, but I will be using their product much more often.  I will go back and buy more, especially for Christmas gifts for my foodie friends.</review>
< name>
Timothy Riley< /name>

<time>1513579315663< /time><Name>debra Wright< /Name><Rate>5<//Rate>< Resp>

<pics>None< /pics></record></dataset><record>
<review>I did not know this place even existed. I was walking in old sac with my niece. We were going to leave until I saw this place.  I went in and saw that they sell flavored olive oils and balsamic vinegars...OMG

I tasted many flavors. Some I personally did not like...but others blew my tongue away...

I reduce balsamic and make a glaze to put over beets and other things...now these flavors are awesome.

I loved the raspberry...black cherry...grapefruit...maple...but my favorite was the blackberry ginger. I ended up buying a 750 ml bottle.

The vinegar...they have red and white..I believe the white is 12 year...and the red 18 year...and the flavor...it is quality stuff...

The staff was so friendly and helpful.  They will give you a punch card after you buy so many bottles valued at 20 dollars or higher they will give you a 750 ml bottle free...a value of around 38.00 including tax.

The man at the register suggested trying the blackberry over ice cream..
Omg...on the way home stopped to get vanilla bean ice cream...and it taste even better...I could not believe it. I made my niece a funnel cake with ice cream and drizzled this over it...so good.

For the olive oil..they have many flavors...butter flavor is really good. They have little pieces of bread to dip and try the oil. They have flavors like garlic...harissa...blood orange...Persian lime....cilantro...ect.

Look at my pics for different flavors.

God willing I will be back for more.

P.s. if you take your used bottle back..they will give you a dollar discount or 2 dollars on Tuesday.<//review><GmapID>0x809ad6cd1412990b:0x8a3bf3c385b92227< /GmapID>< pictures>

<Text>All I can say is RIBS!!

This place has great ribs.  If you like super tender ribs, this place is for you.  The sauce is a bit tangy and sweet, which must be the Kansas City style of sauce, if so, call me a fan of KC BBQ.

Although everything else on the menu is decent, I wouldn't say it stands out as much as the ribs.  I tend to prefer the long-end ribs.  They are meatier and fattier..hehe... The times I've been here, the brisket has been either hit or miss.  The beef links were good.  You get a lot of bread to slop up the excess sauce on your plate, which is a great thing because when you have so much meat, the added starch is a welcome break.  Sides were good too.

One note of caution is that if you're not a fan of tang in your food, this might not be the best place for you<//Text><userid>111129052490865933911<//userid>< gmapID>

<response>None< /response><rating>4< /rating>< Review>
The choice for me was chicken and links. Just ok but edible. A little on the dry side. The sauce tasty but I had better. Beans just ok and potato salad need more help.

What I was taken in on were the historical pictures of African Americans from years past that decorated the walls. For me it told a story of our past here in America and how we survived those most horrible conditions and were able to come out on the other side battered, bruised but still with our dignity.

I will give them another shot at the dinner plate but will always return to receive more of that precious history that gives us the strength to move forward with our heads up.<//Review>

<rating>5</rating><Review>I was out enjoying the sun when the emotion of hunger hit my mid torso. I was on foot and just happened to be at the Bank of America on San Pablo Ave in Berkeley. Not directly across the street but within a normal persons field of vision I spot KC Barbeque and the picture of slice beef ran untethered through my hungry being. It wasn't a second thought I made my way into and ordered a slice beef dinner to go. To my palates enjoyment the beef was tender and well smoked with nice flavored edges, the sauce was delicate and sweet just enough spice paired with chunky potato salad, baked beans and three pieces of bread. Before I could make it up the block I had already slipped the most available piece of the beef from the heavy box and into my mouth at that point it hit me that this meal had to be enjoyed with a premium beer; I'm talking anyone of your local craft beers. Why? This bar-b-que was too tasty for Bud, Miller and Heineken.<//Review>< Pictures>

< text>
As of July 2017, this is a pretty new Motel 6; at least, the interior is new.

It was nice not to have ash trays in the room, finally! There was a very slight tobacco odor, though. It was not bad, but there were two cigarette burns on the tub. Some people just don't obey the rules!

Many of the bright-white towels had some type of mark on them. I suppose it is really hard to get stains out of white towels. They were grey and another had bright red fingernail polish on it.

The pool was not finished; but, I suppose it will be, soon.

There is a security guard during the day; but, they really need one at night to keep the locals from roaming through the parking lot. One guy was collecting cans at 4:30 in the morning. I do not begrudge him his living, but I don't like having to watch my car at that time. (I wish the motel had a recycling bin, too.)

On the plus side, I do like the new recessed lighting; it's very nice and contemporary!

The front desk people were very nice, letting us check in early. Thank you!< /text>

<Name>Lance Hotz< /Name><date>1521984651526<//date>< Rate>
3<//Rate>
< Text>
This is going to be long and I apologize. If you only plan to spend two or three nights then this is a good place for you. If you are looking for a homey kind of room and planning for a longer stay you might need to look elsewhere. But please keep in mind this is a budget motel. Even with the negatives I would give this location three and a half stars.

My wife and I had to rent a motel room for several days while waiting for our new residence to be ready.
We chose Motel Six because it was pet friendly for our little dog. This Motel Six is not in the best area, with working girls around and doing what working girls do. However within the motel area we did feel secure. The room we stayed in was a very large corner room, over 200 square feet. The rooms have been recently remodeled and now they don't exactly shout "Welcome." Hospital sterile is not a good look, seriously.

The only things that break up the monotonous  walls are the window, an air conditioner, and a nice sized flat screen TV. There were no wall mounted lamps next to the large king size bed, not even the mandatory tacky artwork on the walls. The ceiling lighting is in keeping with the room design, recessed, white, and sterile, as if the designers didn't know they make flourescent light bulbs that duplicate the warm welcome feeling of the incandescent ones. In fact I even brought one of my own lamps from home.

The clothes hanging rack is miniscule, just two small posts protruding from the wall with not enough room between them to allow the hangers not to overlap each other. If you have more than eight items of clothing to hang I am afraid you are out of luck. Below that are three small shelves, the only places in this very large room to put folding clothes. Both of these will be an issue for any guy who has a wife or a girlfriend.

This leads to the lack of surfaces. There is a half table mounted to the wall along with two Spartan Ikea type chairs. The bathroom sink area didn't need to have such a small surface area, as to one side there was a fifteen inch empty space between it and the adjacent wall. Again remember the wives and girlfriends. There is no dresser or chest of drawers as is found in most motel rooms to store your clothes, thus there is no top surface on which to set anything either. In summary it is as if Motel 6 did the remodel on the cheap with no thought toward the convenience and comfort of its customers, especially leaving out wives and girlfriends.

That is too bad, since the staff there is great. I had no problems with the rudeness of the housekeeping staff of which other reviewers have mentioned. And if I did I wouldn't hold it against them. They are working at a hard minimum wage job, often with no tips for their good service. And the office staff are all very nice people, always willing to help with a friendly smile and that is a huge plus for travelers. I just wish that in this case at least Motel Six was on par with its employees.
PS: On the plus side Motel Six provides in room mini refrigerators. üòÅüòÅüòÅ< /Text>
